document level embedding ^9Gl58ICp

 ^6ya6ejK0

1. collect all file names from a directory (done)
2. embed each file name (done) ... add each result to qdrant
3. embed our query (done) ... run qdrant search
4. choose the closest K matches (done)
5. go into those files and embed the documents text (as sentence level embeddings)
    5a. chunk if required (>= TOKEN_THRESHOLD)
6. choose the best match per document ^YmfnrOsU
